First of all, in terms of price, let‚Äôs talk about the toiletries provided by the hotel, the luggage tag with the logo, the mini bar with rich soft drinks and snacks included in the package, the drop-off service, the pick-up and drop-off within three kilometers, the 500 yuan consumption limit in the package, two servings The Michelin-quality breakfast and the room upgrade coupon are worth half the price. The second is the hotel's service. Combined with the "Thousand Miles a Day" trip to Universal Studios and the Forbidden City in the past two days, the bad weather and heavy traffic made my mood hit rock bottom. However, from the concierge to the front desk to the restaurant waiter and the housekeeper, I felt the human touch and warmth of the city of Beijing and the sense of brand belonging of Bulgari employees. Every employee's face is filled with confidence, their behavior is dignified and elegant. In particular, CUE the housekeeper HELEN. After checking in, he gave a detailed introduction to the hotel's overview, the business hours of various locations, and recommended nearby restaurants. He was responsive to requests and responded very quickly. He was extremely professional but did not feel any sense of distance at all. He is his friend in Beijing, and he is fully worthy of being Bulgari‚Äôs signature brand. What moved and surprised me the most was that I didn‚Äôt expect to find a photo of us from my girlfriend‚Äôs circle of friends and print it out and put it in a photo frame. It was really thoughtful. I will be able to savor this wonderful experience for a long time to come. I think this is effective communication, a way to capture what they care about and like from the chat with the guests. I have every reason to believe that even if they can't take selfies or group photos, they will have many other ways to impress the guests, because as long as You can get sincerity with sincerity. In fact, this is the difference between top luxury and high luxury. At a certain level, everyone's hardware conditions are similar. What matters is the employees' understanding of the service. We also welcome HELEN housekeepers to contact us if they come to Shanghai to travel after seeing this comment, so as to show their kindness to the landlord. Whether as a hotel enthusiast, a circle member, or a tourist, we sincerely invite everyone to truly experience the uniqueness of Bulgari. It is true that many people will define it as a gathering place for Internet celebrities, but they still hope that hotel employees like HELEN Butler, who are unknown but exude infinite light, can be perceived and understood by everyone. I am willing to work harder in life and see you again in the future!
